margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>a) high mp cargoes will freeze   inside and will restrict sampler from going down by gravity. </em></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>b) source of contamination. </em></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>c) ullage for foaming cargoes is   not representative of tank content. </em></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>d) temperature of UTI is not   representative of tank content.</em></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>e) with sediment cargoes UTI   ullage is not accurate. </em></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>g) the wedge formula used for   calculating yard provided ullage tables becomes redundant \u2013as the formula is   based on tape assuming vertical position by gravity. </em></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><em>   </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\n<tr style=\"mso-yfti-irow: 1;\">   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 30%;\" width=\"30%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Substandard condition</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 70%;\" width=\"70%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">20 - Defective equipment,   machinery or tools</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\n<tr style=\"mso-yfti-irow: 2;\">   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 30%;\" width=\"30%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Personal factors</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 70%;\" width=\"70%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">05 - Lack of knowledge</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\n<tr style=\"mso-yfti-irow: 3;\">   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 30%;\" width=\"30%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Job factors</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 70%;\" width=\"70%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">09 - Inadequate design</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\n<tr style=\"mso-yfti-irow: 4;\">   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 30%;\" width=\"30%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Control action failure</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 70%;\" width=\"70%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">01 - Leadership and administration   - A: Inadequate requirements/guidelines</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\n<tr style=\"mso-yfti-irow: 5;\">   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 30%;\" width=\"30%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Action</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 70%;\" width=\"70%\"></td>  </tr>\n<tr style=\"mso-yfti-irow: 6; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;\">   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 30%;\" width=\"30%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Suggested preventive/corrective   actions</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>   <td style=\"background-color: transparent; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 0.75pt; width: 70%;\" width=\"70%\"><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">ALL XXX TANKERS WHO HAVE UTI TUBE   EXTENSIONS TO BE SLOTTED OR PERFORATED--&nbsp;&nbsp; THIS MEANS DOZENS OF HOLES ON ENTIRE   LENGTH--&nbsp; NOT JUST ONE OR TWO ON TOP.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; THERE MUST BE AT LEAST ONE INCH ENTRY   CLEARANCE AT THE BOTTOM .</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div></td>  </tr>\n</tbody></table><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0BGvYP5Cigw/TpqlteR5Z1I/AAAAAAAAHB4/syiww5id_QM/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0BGvYP5Cigw/TpqlteR5Z1I/AAAAAAAAHB4/syiww5id_QM/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n29 YEARS IN COMMAND</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "12", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/3142929632955684653/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4352854725930933557", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-10-14T13:39:00+05:30", "updated": "2011-10-14T13:39:38+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzE4NTc5Nzc4Njg0Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/10/commercial-matters-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4352854725930933557", "title": "COMMERCIAL MATTERS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Zzqbop-7KrQ/Tpftot-FKzI/AAAAAAAAG_g/nzsOCZi5NYs/s1600/xxc.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Zzqbop-7KrQ/Tpftot-FKzI/AAAAAAAAG_g/nzsOCZi5NYs/s1600/xxc.png\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: left;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\">COMMERCIAL<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>MATTERS<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Read the charter party . Check out the time allowed for a full load. What is the minimum rate for a chemical parcel. The 100 psi or 7 kg manifold pressure rule applies for what minimum quantity limit of parcel. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Parcel chemicals which are in an obviously dangerous condition and which could damage the ship, its tanks or adjacent chemicals must NEVER be loaded. (For example you are aware that an Ammonia based inhibitor has been used for stabilizing a polymerizing chemical <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>which was stored in a Zinc Silicate tank ashore ). <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Hence on chemical tankers it is important to observe correct sampling procedures. It is important to know what type of pump is used for loading. If the pump is not a piston pump or screw pump it should be possible to take a first foot line sample in a clear SELF SEALING glass bottle against a closed manifold valve. If the shore / barge line content is contaminated<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>or has water this fact can easily be found out . Sample bottle label must contain ships name/ voyage number/ date/ location / type of sample manifold, tank . Samples must be retained for one year. It is important to drain compressed air lines before any line blow. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Often shippers misdeclare the loading temperatures of high melting point cargoes which are brought in by rail wagons. Chemicals which is not in a condition as projected in the shipping documents must be rejected. It is understood that the ship staff are not experts with regard to quality of cargo but he can observe any reasonable obvious deviations like rancid odour veg oils, foaming Molasses , milky DIDP/DINP , non sputtering Sulphuric acid or barge dischg with open ullaging / veg oil sweeping in heavy rain.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If you suspect inherent vice even an ordinary letter of protest will serve the purpose.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">No documents must be signed for any cargo which is not yet on board. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Stowage must be planned meticulously for parcel cargoes and don\u2019t allow the charterers to rush you into immediate stowage solutions without double checking. On parcel tankers there are more than one hundred considerations before you arrive at the best stowage from all perspectives. It is important that you are not hustled into accepting only the sub-charterers perspective.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">All tanks must be inspected prior hose connection. Fill up the proper enclosed space checklist. If a tank has been methanol sprayed<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>or methanol dehumidified the surveyor will want a Draeger ppm reading of the tank to be wall washed. A tank cannot be entered by a shore person unless a ships officer is present. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Unless expressly advised tanks must be cleaned to water white standard dry and odor free. Unseen areas are checked by rubbing hands for residues\u2014especially under steam coils and impeller area ( for hyd oil) . On epoxy ships the tank coating<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>must be 98.5% intact and flaked coating must be removed and checked for cargo residue behind coating. There should be no loose scale or rust. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">For heated cargoes heating coils must be tested applying full steam pressure for AT LEAST TWENTY MINUTES. If any leaks are detected the tank should not be used until \u201cpermanent\u201d repairs are carried out and retested again.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>No soft patches are allowed even with heat/ chemical resistant putties. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Vapor return spools can be connected only if it is the same homogeneous grade in all tanks. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Look into manifold lines for cleanliness before the shore surveyor does. No manifold hoses can be rigged unless a manifold rigging plan has been signed by the chief officer and posted in the CCR and a copy is given to the deck watch. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">To remove moisture from pipelines to handle moisture sensitive cargoes like DINP/ DIDP/ MEG FG etc blow all lines with nitrogen till the last drain valve at pumpstack is completely moisture free. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Shore line is usually pigged. It is a good practice to inspect the pig if feasible and permitted to see if is free of moisture, odour and cargo residues. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If the ship\u2019s crew is constrained to connect shore loading hoses, a letter of protest should be issued before the job stating that \u201cship/ owner/ crew/ charterer cannot be held responsible for any incident or direct / indirect liability that may arise due to the ships involvement in the connection/ disconnection\u201d. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Do not disconnect hoses unless you get the tank dry certificate at disport. Like wise do not start loading at loadport unless the tank ready certificate is recd on board. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">When ever a first foot tank sample is taken make a log entry. There is no need to take first foot samples on ships initiative unless required by EMS Singapore office. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If there is foam on top of cargo issue a LOP. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Separate pumping<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>log must be made for each grade. Otherwise it becomes difficult to collect demurrage.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If ships discharge is restricted by shore with a pressure of less than 7,0 kgs / 100 psi, or the rate of which the vessel can discharge the entire load within 24 hrs, a LOP must be issued. The vessel must always discharge with a min. pressure of 7,0 kgs (universal c/party requirement engraved in stone ) at the manifold. If not doing so, the reason must be clearly remarked in the pumping log.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Whenever pre-wash is required according to Marpol regulations and washings are discharged ashore the pre-wash record should be made and attached to the vessel\u2019s slop record.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 170.1pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Cargo</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">: Chemical name. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 170.1pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Tank</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">: Identity of tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">In case ships figure is greater than shore figure do not protest unless you have confirmed with the operator.<span style=\"color: black;\"> It may be better to sacrifice<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>extra freight when pitted against the option of being slapped with imaginary and deliberate shortage claims. If the outturn quantity at disport is more extra freight can be claimed even in the absence of a LOP for discrepancy .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 170.1pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">During the voyage the cargo temperatures for heated cargoes of each tank must be checked at least twice a day.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The average temperature is to be used in the heating report. There must be one heating report for each grade.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Any delays which can affect laytime counting, must be recorded under delays / remarks.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">A draft survey is normally conducted when it is impossible to obtain the density of the cargo.<br />\nThe draft survey should be done as accurately as possible as the outcome of the draft survey often is used as Bill of Lading figure. If vessel is rolling slightly mention it in the ullage sheet and SOF remark column. If the draft survey has been conducted incorrectly, the Owners may face a claim from the consignee. Density of dock water must be ascertained for 4 metres below waterlevel.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Combined masters certificate is required by many shippers, when vegoils are carried in accordance with FOSFA rules.The certificate should only be issued if required by the shipper / surveyor or charterer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The Master must convey the tankcleaning plan after departure discharge port. The tanklcleaning done report must be completed as per format and filed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">AGENTS:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Agents are paid to board the vessel daily . In some notorious ports protective agents are used by the charterers to expedite ships operations.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Relevant messages must hence be copied to them especially NOR. Ask agents for pre arrival information well in advance and not at the last minute.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">NOTE: PORT LOG must contain tankwise start/ stop/ sweep/ line blow.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Remember a ships delay is a delay ONLY if it interferes with the charterers business. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Detention due to inherent vice of cargo is NOT OFFHIRE.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">SBT ballasting / deballasting times must NEVER be mentioned in SOF.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">LAYDAYS:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">It is the period of time the owner will keep his ship available for loading/ dischg without fines. LAYCAN is the agreed date of loading. It is charterers duty to load/ dischg cargo within 72 hours after laycan. If vessel is not ready within 1600 hours of the last day then charterers may cancel.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div style=\"background: rgb(248, 252, 255); line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">There is no obligation on the charterers to load a vessel that arrived before the commencement of laydays, but if they did, they could not normally expect to use the vessel without paying for it.</span></div><div style=\"background: rgb(248, 252, 255); line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">MANIFEST:</span></span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If the agent does not give customs manifest then use ships form.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Certain ports like in Italy require manifest for \u201cin transit \u201c or \u201c same bottom\u201d cargoes too.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">DEADFREIGHT:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">When a charterer agrees to load a ship with FULL cargo and then fails to do so\u2014the difference between the quantity shipped and the quantity the ship is capable of loading may be recoverable as deadfreight. If the ship is cubed out\u2014the fact must be mentioned as a remark in the SOF. Dead freight claims are not discrepancy protests,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>It is also possible that one parcel may be subject to both deadfreight and discrepancy claims.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">COMMINGLING CLAUSE:</span></span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">It is commonplace for one chemical parcel to be sold to various consignees each of whom receive a portion of the total quantity loaded. In such cases the total quantity of all the b/l issued must equal the total loaded and each b/l must contain the following commingling clause.\u2014\u2018 this shipment was loaded on board the ship as part of one original lot of ----- mtons with no segregation as to the parcels. Neither the ship nor the owners assume any responsibilities for the consequences of such commingling nor the separation thereof at the time of delivery\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">All our company&nbsp;ships are equipped with a digital camera which can be used in the video mode. When ever you feel live documentation of an event is required to prevent your ship from losing money use it. This must be with the Master in port and must be readily available at a few seconds notice , say to Chief officer or Duty officer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Sometimes the tank surveyor rejects the tank or does a wall wash as a delaying manoevere because cargo is not ready or a chemical barge is arriving late. If the master suspects such a thing, protest and if required call P&amp;I.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">SURVEYORS:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">In certain small ports one single surveyor wear different hats. Like in the good old days Penavico China was agent for every body. The master should be sensitive to the potential of such conflict of interests. P&amp;I surveyors can attend to the vessel for cargo contamination, damage to jetty, pollution , third party damages and investigations into sea worthiness of ship in the context of General average. The P&amp;I surveyor can be head owners or time charterers. Most reputed parcel chemical time charterers have their own P&amp;I to handle cargo related matters. The master must be aware whom the surveyor represents. Surveyors acting on behalf of third parties such as charterers, receivers, terminal, stevedores and other ships must be treated with utmost caution.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Master should be careful about release of information and documents. Managers and owners should be informed so that they can arrange a surveyor to represent their interests before the other nuisance potential surveyor is permitted to carry out his business. Master should not feel embarrassed about speaking privately with owners surveyor even if it means that he has to tell the other surveyor to step out into the alleyway. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">SAMPLING:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If there is a cargo contamination claim the Master must: <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Immediately call in the local representative of the vessel\u2019s P&amp;I club.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Notify Operator about the alleged claim and confirm that the P&amp;I representative is attending.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">and not hand them to anyone, except in agreement with the P&amp;I representative, and only against written receipt.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Master IS NOT obliged to follow any orders that go beyond the terms of the charter party.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The Master must NEVER load any cargo which is not on the coating resistance list and the certificate of fitness.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If the charterers inspector rejects the tanks and as a master you feels cheated ( because cargo is not ready or whatever), approach P&amp;I to appoint an independent surveyor.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">LOP<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If ship cannot discharge the whole cargo in 24 hrs or maintain 100 psi at the rail throughout\u2014the MUST be LOP covering the delay or all rights are automatically waived. Delay in receiving shore documents after disconnection of hoses must be documented. Any document on which shore signature could not be obtained must be endorsed accordingly. Delays between tendering NOR and berthing should be documented.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Master to protest if the latest ASTM tables<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>6A and 24A are not used for oils / cargo surveyors not using own or standard equipment.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">IWL<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">An IWL chart is attached which should be displayed on the Bridge or ships Office. This clearly shows the areas outside the IWL and the areas which are seasonal exclusions. The map also has a reference, which gives the various positions and dates for the areas excluded and seasonally excluded.<br />\n<br />\nMasters should be aware that a breach of the IWL can invalidate the Hull and Machinery Insurance. To maintain the insurance cover the managers are required to inform the insurers of the IWL breach and dates. The managers may also be required to comply with certain conditions and / or pay an additional premium.<br />\n<br />\nMasters should familiarise themselves with these limits and should it become apparent that they will breach IWL then they should inform this office. Vessels on time charter are sometimes weather routed and advised to proceed on a route, which takes them outside IWL. Although the charter party will contain a clause stating that the vessel is to be always within IWL, the routing company may not be aware of restrictions and it remains the Master\u2019s responsibility to be aware of the situation and inform the managers accordingly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Inform the company and charterers by standard message the date and time in UTC of entering and departing IWL / exclusion zone limits.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Any messages regarding change of disport, quantity of consignee must be copied to charterers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Standard messages must be sent by email or telex<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>but never by fax<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If the master cannot follow the weather routing due to constraint of heating cargo, tankcleaning, repairs on deck etc he must communicate to the weather router through the charterers .<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Ordered speed must be interpreted as the average speed required to be made WP<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Reserve bunkers must take into account boiler consumptions for HO for tankcleaning in cold weather and cargo heating..<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If on any voyage if the heating requirements would cause a vessel to reduce speed, notify the charterers<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The measurement of bulk chemicals is not accurate if ship is rolling slightly at berth and also evaporation losses will occur during a long voyage. Prolonged rolling and pitching during hot heavy weather can increase the rate of evaporation loss of cargo, and may result in voyage transit loss of cargo. To keep measurement inaccuracies to a minimum, standard procedures should be adopted by the chief officer<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>for all measurements of cargo especially if the voyage is long with volatile cargo . It is usual practise for many loadport surveyors to calculate cargo using ASTM mineral oil tables in their laptop computers which will inflate the cargo tonnage on board, when compared to calculations with density correction factor, the way it must be done for non mineral oil chemicals . <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Ullage reports should be signed for \u201cullages and temps only\u201d\u2014all ships must have a stamp made .<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 28.35pt 56.7pt 1.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Non persistent oils: CPP , veg oils and animal oils<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">In some berths masters will be told be charterers to discharge within the tidal window. Master to ensure that the ship is always afloat\u2014if not cast off and berth at the next tidal window.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">At SBM if the ship has any problems keeping engines running astern continiously ( in the absence of a tug ) and inform the charterers .<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The Bareboat/ Time/ Voyage charterer of a vessel who subcharters the vessel to another party is known as the <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">disponent owner </b>in the new charter agreement.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Composite cargoes: 2 or more grades having widely differing specs if carried on the same ship eg lub oils and white products<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">TANK CLEANING &amp; SLOP DISPOSAL</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Master must discharge as much slops as possible enroute after tankcleaning. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">During tankcleaning ensure that you must ensure that you follow the Marpol regulations with respect to special areas, depth of water, distance from land etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The Master should always contact his Operator should he be in doubt whether the wash water can be discharged to the sea.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The master must give the operator enough time to react to arrange for slops to be landed at a feasible port.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Disposal of slops containing tankcleaning chemicals, can be expensive as this is deemed as chemical waste.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">So it is important that the Operator is <st1:personname w:st=\"on\">info</st1:personname>rmed about the type and quantity of chemicals  inherent in the slops.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">The Master must <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">never </b>on his own<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"> </b>arrange landing of tankcleaning slops, unless written <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>statement is received from the terminal/ agent that it is free of charge.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Landing of slops always must be arranged through Operator. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 7.8in 8.3in 8.8in; This crude divine diamond Syamantakam used to glow even in the dark.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QRszmtzEgc0/TpbDx1j_CjI/AAAAAAAAG8o/n4rZ0fLt01k/s1600/imagesCAYSOEGM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QRszmtzEgc0/TpbDx1j_CjI/AAAAAAAAG8o/n4rZ0fLt01k/s1600/imagesCAYSOEGM.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nToday this naively cut for style ( totally screwed by British ) is on the British Crown as Kohinoor--stolen property on a national emblem!. In 1997 when Queen Elizabeth 2 came to India , the Indian Parliament requested her to return this dimond which has great sentimental value in India as Lord Krishna is a god. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red; font-size: x-large;\">She told us to FO!</span><br />\n<br />\nSince this diamond had been set into the British crown, Britain has known zilch good luck. There is a curse attached to the diamond, that only gods and women can wear it with impunity.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hro62KA5J-E/TpbECRCR2BI/AAAAAAAAG9A/nRONg8Ut2ik/s1600/jjjjj.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hro62KA5J-E/TpbECRCR2BI/AAAAAAAAG9A/nRONg8Ut2ik/s640/jjjjj.png\" width=\"331\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe West came to know about Indian diamonds as early as 3000 years ago, when King Solomon imported diamonds via ships going from Kerala.<br />\n<br />\nRATNA PARIKSHA was a 5000 year old Sanskrit text on optics which dealt with critical angles, high refractive index&nbsp;of diamond ( 2.4 ) and low critical angle ( 24 deg ) and &nbsp;total internal reflection physics and the art of cutting diamonds, to make it spit fire. It clearly states that only diamond can cut diamond, hence polishing must be done with diamond , and that if a diamond is cut poorly it will NOT sparkle. <br />\n<br />\nOur 4000 year old Indian temples had pin hole cameras which could give inverted pictures and the coloured prism. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-vdpzWXwR33Q/TpbFPa3aTdI/AAAAAAAAG9g/3LYSW72fKlM/s1600/imagesCA77LE2A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-vdpzWXwR33Q/TpbFPa3aTdI/AAAAAAAAG9g/3LYSW72fKlM/s1600/imagesCA77LE2A.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn the picture above--see the inverted temple gopuram.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JZSdDLFCrjo/TpbFJnyuBwI/AAAAAAAAG9Y/e-nOuz3LCLM/s1600/imagesCA2SS70X.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JZSdDLFCrjo/TpbFJnyuBwI/AAAAAAAAG9Y/e-nOuz3LCLM/s1600/imagesCA2SS70X.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAll this knowledge has been patented by the white man. Even the Indian invention of wheel had been given to Egypt.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/kYnNe-esGvc/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/kYnNe-esGvc&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/kYnNe-esGvc&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nIndian diamond cutters are so reliable that even today in 2011 that nearly 1.45 million cutters still cut 13 out of 14 diamonds world wide( &nbsp;93.5% by numbers cut )--despite the inroads of computer controlled laser cutting technology.. <br />\n<br />\nIn India if you buy a diamond and if the stone brings bad luck to you, you can go and return it. No questions will be asked--for a full refund.<br />\n<br />\nIndians as usual developed their Vedic knowledge by observing nature. We still have the&nbsp;most extensive flora and fauna on the planet. Total internal reflection, refraction and refractive index was found by observing rainbows at waterfalls.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-aQzKpw7vLJA/TpbFkrK6_II/AAAAAAAAG9w/fetWJ5Aj0Ho/s1600/imagesCANE6RZ1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-aQzKpw7vLJA/TpbFkrK6_II/AAAAAAAAG9w/fetWJ5Aj0Ho/s1600/imagesCANE6RZ1.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\nRainbow, is seen usually in the sky opposite to the Sun at the end of a shower and also in the spray of waterfalls. In the primary bow, the colours are arranged with the red outside. Above the perfect bow is a secondary bow, in which the colours are arranged in reverse order; this bow is dimmer, because of a double internal reflection within the drops. </div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--5dDS3ybsM8/TpbFe3kpGII/AAAAAAAAG9o/9VEtrpa4IMo/s1600/imagesCAJLGIGJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"298\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--5dDS3ybsM8/TpbFe3kpGII/AAAAAAAAG9o/9VEtrpa4IMo/s400/imagesCAJLGIGJ.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\nWhen the sunlight enters a raindrop it is refracted&nbsp;by, and reflected from, the drop in such a way that the light appears as a spectrum of colours. When the Sun is low in the sky the rainbow appears relatively high; as the Sun rises higher, the rainbow appears lower in the sky, maintaining the critical 40\u00b0- to 42\u00b0-angle. When the Sun is more than 42\u00b0 above the horizon no rainbow can be seen because the required angle passes over the head of the observer.  </div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-54EqpTr_0t0/TpbFtpcTJBI/AAAAAAAAG94/TfiEAIOSCp4/s1600/imagesCAZZ32LL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-54EqpTr_0t0/TpbFtpcTJBI/AAAAAAAAG94/TfiEAIOSCp4/s1600/imagesCAZZ32LL.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The secondary rainbow has an angular radius of about 50\u00b0 and hence is seen outside of the primary bow.&nbsp; Higher-order rainbows, resulting from three or more internal reflections, are exceedingly weak but can be&nbsp;observed&nbsp;in Kerala in the months of August.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p>  <em><span style=\"color: blue;\">LORE :</span></em></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Surya the Sun God gave Satrajit, of Dwaraka , the Syamanataka diamond as he was pleased with his devotion. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Satrajit's brother Prasena wore the jewel on his neck and went for a hunt. He climbed a tree waiting for some game, a lion came by and just as Prasena was about to shoot it, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>when a <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>snake, dropped from a branch above . Startled he fell from the tree. As he was falling, the necklace with the Syamantaka gem got caught in a branch and Prasena hung by the neck, and was killed instantly.<o:p></o:p></span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Now the lion below, being attracted to the glow of the gem, picked it up and carried it away. As the lion walked away with the gem, Jambavan the king of the bears saw him. Being hypnotized <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>by the glow of the gem, he attacked the lion and killed it and took the gem to his cave and gifted it to his infant son.<o:p></o:p></span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Prasena did not return to Dwarka and people were wondering what had happened to him. Satrajit suspected that Krishna might have killed Prasena in order to attain the gem. Krishna, in order to prove his innocence, gathered a search party and went into the forest.<o:p></o:p></span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">A few hours later, they found Prasena's body. Krishna noticed lion tracks around the body and assumed that a lion must have killed Prasena. On following the lion tracks, they came across the body of the dead lion. Krishna noticed that the lion was mauled by bear's claws and noticed that there were bear tracks around the body. On following the bear tracks Krishna reached Jambavan's cave. Krishna sensing the danger ordered the rest of the party to stay outside while he entered the cave alone. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Krishna found Jambavan's son playing with the Syamantaka gem. Frightened by the stranger, Jambavan's son let out a wail that alerted Jambavan. Now Jambavan thought someone was attacking his child and attacked Krishna. Krishna fought Jambavan for twenty-eight days after which Jambavan recognised Krishna's divinity and surrendered to him. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DNNumgPxxHg/TpkOZlurPxI/AAAAAAAAHAY/qxA5vPU3QFY/s1600/imagesCA3EGHKM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DNNumgPxxHg/TpkOZlurPxI/AAAAAAAAHAY/qxA5vPU3QFY/s1600/imagesCA3EGHKM.jpg\" /></span></em></a></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Along with the gem, Jambavan offered Krishna his beautiful daughter Jambavati's hand in marriage. <o:p></o:p></span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: red;\">TILL 1886--EVERY SINGLE DIAMOND SEEN ABROAD WAS STOLEN FROM INDIA , FOR INDIANS ARE NOT IN THE HABIT OF SELLING DIVINE DIAMONDS .</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pyE91PYQeRY/Tp2e3qrGxxI/AAAAAAAAHEY/uoPL9ayRwFk/s1600/rrrr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"204\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pyE91PYQeRY/Tp2e3qrGxxI/AAAAAAAAHEY/uoPL9ayRwFk/s320/rrrr.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\nThe great Orlov diamond of 190 carats set on the Imperial sceptre of Catherine the Great of Russia was initially 3 times bigger--or the size of a large hen's egg. </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oXfzfIT8bQU/Tp2fckerkRI/AAAAAAAAHFA/MoHAN0OdWHA/s1600/200px-Orloff_copy.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oXfzfIT8bQU/Tp2fckerkRI/AAAAAAAAHFA/MoHAN0OdWHA/s1600/200px-Orloff_copy.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n&nbsp;It was just one of a pair, which formed&nbsp;the eyes of the ancient Vishnu idol at Sri Ranganathaswamy temple , at Srirangam , 3 kms north of&nbsp; Tiruchinapalli, Tamil Nadu, India. </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HR1xoHYfH2Y/Tp2fUIPr5OI/AAAAAAAAHE4/RD0EQAtW35U/s1600/tt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Originally it was 200 carats.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JfVfUOBIlK4/Tp2fi4qxZLI/AAAAAAAAHFI/l8NmNypjMKg/s1600/untitledqqq.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"173\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JfVfUOBIlK4/Tp2fi4qxZLI/AAAAAAAAHFI/l8NmNypjMKg/s200/untitledqqq.png\" width=\"200\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">This huge priceless divine diamond&nbsp;was cut into three to cure a curse attached to the diamond.
