Baker knows he is dying and he stumbles away from the shoot out and begins the slow walk towards the&nbsp;sunset, to a stream. &nbsp;His wife sees him take his final steps and lets out a mournful wail. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">This walk describing the feelings of a dying sheriff , is set to the strains of Bob Dylan's famous classic song-- Knockin' on heavens door.</span> </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/EEo8obsERSQ/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/EEo8obsERSQ&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/EEo8obsERSQ&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The video below gives the lyrics--but it is sung by Guns and Roses. An enduring song for the ages.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/y864fRVBh24/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/y864fRVBh24&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/y864fRVBh24&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Director Sam Peckinpah, made a classic movie. He was an alcoholic and had a king sized ego. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Why not?&nbsp; He was good!.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dSD66Sg7IOw/TpU5StDsThI/AAAAAAAAG6g/fowDFqOoS5w/s1600/imagesCAYLAV8A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dSD66Sg7IOw/TpU5StDsThI/AAAAAAAAG6g/fowDFqOoS5w/s1600/imagesCAYLAV8A.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">He clashed constantly during the making of the movie with James Aubrey, the powerful head of MGM, who wanted to micro-manage and cut down costs, giving him unskilled local staff from Mexico. &nbsp;As a result the movie finished 3 weeks behind schedule and overshot the budget. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The vindictive Aubrey, who had no artistic imagination, ruined the editing , cut off 18 full minutes of crucial scenes, which made Peckinpah sue MGM and demand&nbsp;that his name be removed from the movie credits. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Q0yX1Ie1Y5Y/TpU5OYsGQ6I/AAAAAAAAG6Y/oUr0-D35JlY/s1600/imagesCALY3LUC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Q0yX1Ie1Y5Y/TpU5OYsGQ6I/AAAAAAAAG6Y/oUr0-D35JlY/s1600/imagesCALY3LUC.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Aubrey with a monster sized ego, was the type of hard nosed number crunching guy who would tell an artist or a musician \"harder, faster\". This clash of personalities caused Aubrey to score brownie points , rape the movie, and it bombed at the box office. No wonder Aubrey's nick name was \" the smiling cobra\".&nbsp; Straight talkin' Lucille Ball used to refer to him as a SOB every time.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fKc9PN7MBP8/TpU5W-EWfQI/AAAAAAAAG6o/7CZzZ0-vsJA/s1600/billy2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"262\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fKc9PN7MBP8/TpU5W-EWfQI/AAAAAAAAG6o/7CZzZ0-vsJA/s320/billy2.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">15 years later, in 1988 Turner Home Entertainment on popular demand re-edited the whole movie, the way Sam Peckinpah would have wanted it, and the result was a classic masterpiece. This included the sequence where an aged Pat Garrett was ambushed and killed-and as we hear this gunfire, the movie flashes back to Billy the Kid--all with the soulful strains of Bob Dylan's&nbsp;twang..</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-urZB2MCAfhA/TpU5dAqgCfI/AAAAAAAAG6w/EZm1YUzC_3o/s1600/nnnv.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-urZB2MCAfhA/TpU5dAqgCfI/AAAAAAAAG6w/EZm1YUzC_3o/s320/nnnv.jpg\" width=\"236\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Here is the true story--</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Pat Garrett worked as a cowboy and buffalo hunter before becoming a Sheriff. The kid was his partner rider as a cowpoke. He had a reputation as a hot-tempered man, and in 1877 he killed a friend in a drunken brawl, but was acquitted on grounds of self-defense. Garrett then came to Roswell, New Mexico, where he was elected sheriff of Lincoln County in 1880. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Motivated by either a love of justice or the $500 bounty on Billy the Kid, Garrett tracked down two of the Kid's cohorts, Charles Bowdre and Tom O'Folliard, and killed them in Stinking Springs, New Mexico. Then he cornered and arrested Billy the Kid, and brought him to trial on charges of murder. After a speedy trial, the eminent outlaw was ordered to hang, but escaped from jail instead, killing two guards in the process. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">It was rumoured that Pat Garrett had deliberately kept a gun for the Kid to escape in the toilet. <span class=\"description1\"><span style=\"color: windowtext; font-style: normal; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Garrett was conveniently away from Lincoln on county business when the Kid made his escape. Rather than chase after the fugitive, Garrett kept to his ranch mending fences and attending to his cattle. In July, the Sheriff received word that the Kid was hiding out at the abandoned Fort Sumner about 140 miles west of Lincoln. Rounding up two of his deputies, John Poe and Thomas McKinney, Garrett set off in pursuit of the Kid</span></span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">So pretty soon Garrett set out after his former friend. Using a mutual acquaintance to arrange a meeting on 14 July 1881, Garrett crouched in a dark room waiting for the outlaw's arrival. As soon as the door opened, Garrett shot Billy the Kid dead without a word. The truth is he shot someone else by mistake and got him buried in haste without following accepted and lawful police procedures, in between his fallen companions Tom O Folliard and Charlie Bowdre. A single tombastone was used for all 3 , with a one word epitaph \"pals\" engraved in it.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Some hailed him as a hero for ending a famous criminal's life, but others called him a coward for the manner in which he lured and killed the fugitive, who was a dear friend before . Amid these whispers and aspersions, Garrett soon left his job as sheriff. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After a few years as a lawman in another county, Garrett was appointed by President Theodore Roosevelt to supervise the El Paso office of the Customs Department. Known as a gambler, heavy drinker and supremely arrogant , he <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>did not last long in this job either. He then quit law enforcement, and lived on a ranch with his wife and nine children, where he was generally unpopular among the locals. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Unable to make the ranch a profitable concern, he leased it to one Wayne Brazel. Soon, however, Garrett decided that he did not approve of the way Brazel was running the ranch, with goats instead of cows, which would lower its value-- and began pressuring Brazel to leave the premises. On 29 February 1908, in a heated discussion, Garrett is said to have told Brazel he would get him off the ranch, \"one way or another\".</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Garrett then turned his back to his tenant, unzipped his pants and began to take a leak, and he was shot twice and killed. Brazel claimed self-defense, the trial lasted one day, and the jury already having pre-conceived notions that Pat was a bad man , deliberated for less than half an hour before finding him not guilty. A huge barbecue was held at another nearby ranch, to celebrate the verdict.</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xXotMa5fbAk/TpU6VRpISXI/AAAAAAAAG74/Z28eRsnDP44/s1600/rws.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"261\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xXotMa5fbAk/TpU6VRpISXI/AAAAAAAAG74/Z28eRsnDP44/s320/rws.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Everyone knew that Pat Garret had warned old buddy outlaw Billy to stay away from him, lest he kills him in the discharge of his duties--but the kid ignored him. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The kid died at the age of 21, and is was rumoured that he killed 21 men--one for every day of his life. But the kid was loved by one and all , as he was really not a bad guy, the circumstances forced him to kill.&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Billy worked as a ranch hand for John Tunstall a leader of one faction seeking control of the county. Tunstall befriended the Kid acting in many ways as a surrogate father. Tunstall's ambush and murder in 1878 by a sheriff's posse set the Kid off on a path of revenge. His first victims were the sheriff and his deputy, killed from ambush on the streets of Lincoln.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JK6ssnnXOKg/TpU6NJJRyUI/AAAAAAAAG7w/J91O4xzgH6I/s1600/y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JK6ssnnXOKg/TpU6NJJRyUI/AAAAAAAAG7w/J91O4xzgH6I/s1600/y.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 13.5pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">So--as per lore, on the fateful night of July 14, the Sheriff and his two deputies approached the dusty old Fort now converted to living quarters. The residents were sympathetic to the Kid and the lawmen could extract little information. Garrett decided to seek out an old friend, Peter Maxwell, who might tell him the Kid's whereabouts. As chance would have it, the Kid stumbled right into the Sheriff's hands\u2014or was it so?. </span><o:p></o:p></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Then in 1950, a 91 year old man Brushy Bill popped up and said that he was the real Billy the kid. He had witnessed the shooting of his friend who was buried as the Kid, by Pat Garrett. They were about to have dinner and his friend went to a nearby house where a freshly killed steer was hung to remove some beef to be cooked. Pat Garrett was waiting in ambush in this house.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bb9lzEF9r6w/TpU6H3o5ShI/AAAAAAAAG7o/XPp1AHlvhM0/s1600/ppp.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"226\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bb9lzEF9r6w/TpU6H3o5ShI/AAAAAAAAG7o/XPp1AHlvhM0/s320/ppp.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">This old man showed all his 26 bullet wounds and several knife wound scars on his body, which exactly coincided with records of the Kid. And he also had the two&nbsp;front rabbit&nbsp;teeth of the Kid. He could make his hands smaller than his wrists and remove handcuffs, the way the Kid used to do. All he wanted was a pardon as promised long ago.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">See the video below.--the events are reconstructed by actors.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/bXZMreEBzXA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/bXZMreEBzXA&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/bXZMreEBzXA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In 1949, William Morrison a paralegal located a man in Central Texas named Ollie P. Roberts (nicknamed \"Brushy Bill\"), who claimed to be Billy the Kid and challenged the popular account of the Kid as shot to death by ex-outlaw buddy, Sheriff Pat Garrett.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4OSAjw0kYtc/TpU5-RL8TtI/AAAAAAAAG7g/pzDDUUMlm6o/s1600/imagesCAEDZL97.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4OSAjw0kYtc/TpU5-RL8TtI/AAAAAAAAG7g/pzDDUUMlm6o/s1600/imagesCAEDZL97.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When it came to the events of the night of July 14, 1881, Brushy said that a man named Billy Barlow was killed by Pat Garrett. Barlow, he said, was partially Mexican, had a beard. Brushy had fled Fort Sumner and hidden in Mexico with a tribe of Yaqui Indians for two years, before he returned to the U.S.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iG7nbnuef8g/TpU54xRo0II/AAAAAAAAG7Y/ZbqlKk0t9g0/s1600/imagesCAUCDYJY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iG7nbnuef8g/TpU54xRo0II/AAAAAAAAG7Y/ZbqlKk0t9g0/s1600/imagesCAUCDYJY.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Morrison managed to meet with old friends of Billy -Severo Gallegos, Martile Able, Jose Montoya, and Bill and Sam Jones. The first three all signed legal affidavits attesting to the fact that Brushy Bill and Billy the Kid were one and the same and the Jones brothers, although they did not sign affidavits (claiming they didn\u2019t want to get involved in legal tangles and publicity ) also stated their agreement with this.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gtNGWlTLftU/TpU50s0jthI/AAAAAAAAG7Q/npWPNiJ8mi8/s1600/imagesCAOOY73Y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gtNGWlTLftU/TpU50s0jthI/AAAAAAAAG7Q/npWPNiJ8mi8/s1600/imagesCAOOY73Y.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For the pardon on Nov. 15, 1950. Thomas J. Mabry, governor of New Mexico, agreed to a private hearing with Morrison and Brushy, along with one or two historians of Mabry\u2018s choosing, to be held on Nov. 29.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>When Brushy and Morrison arrived at Mabry\u2019s mansion, they were shocked to see a crowd with several photographers , reporters, armed policemen and hostile Oscar and Jarvis Garrett (Pat\u2019s sons) . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Sns7JKF-1SY/TpU5upcxGoI/AAAAAAAAG7I/1ppUb_hLzpU/s1600/imagesCA2T3VZ9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Sns7JKF-1SY/TpU5upcxGoI/AAAAAAAAG7I/1ppUb_hLzpU/s1600/imagesCA2T3VZ9.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Badly frightened, Brushy suffered a small stroke, and when the questioning began, he failed miserably even to remember Pat Garrett\u2019s name. He completely forgot basic information about himself , and, when he was asked a serious question regarding the past of Billy the Kid, he forgot that as well. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Stating he felt ill, he was eventually taken to another room to lie down. Shortly thereafter, Gov. Mabry made an announcement that he was not going to pardon Brushy, because he did not believe him to be Billy the Kid. A few days later Brushy Bill died of a heart attack.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">This old man with 26 bullet hole scars on his body, and several knife wounds , which matched that of the Kid, knew he was dying and he wanted a clean sheet with his lord, on the day of judgement. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5z3ogHDwWc4/TpU5pkV0R4I/AAAAAAAAG7A/eApEb76FRBk/s1600/imagesCANQ296D.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5z3ogHDwWc4/TpU5pkV0R4I/AAAAAAAAG7A/eApEb76FRBk/s1600/imagesCANQ296D.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">There was no other tangible reason why he would claim to be Billy\u2014common sense dictates. DNA tests have been ruled out as it seems the graveyard of Billy the Kid was awash with flood waters and then all tombstones were lazily reconstructed after two decades. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fTOwxf416og/TpU5is8KBkI/AAAAAAAAG64/orDgYQ8Os1U/s1600/Brushyindeath.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"235\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fTOwxf416og/TpU5is8KBkI/AAAAAAAAG64/orDgYQ8Os1U/s320/Brushyindeath.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Well this mystery keeps the \u201c Billy the Kid \u201c tourism industry alive. This is what is used in cars for gearbox transmissions.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/rIkroVwOxOs/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/rIkroVwOxOs&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/rIkroVwOxOs&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div><br />\nWhen I was writing a SMS manual for my company at Singapore, I suddenly felt the need to have some inspiration. <br />\n<br />\nI wonder if you understand what this word inspiration can mean or do.<br />\n<br />\nTwo decades&nbsp;ago, one of my Marine Superintendent friends , took me to his home in Mumbai. He wanted me to meet his 16 year old son , and read his poetry.&nbsp; Though he had got his poems vetted by some Hi Fi internationally famous poets&nbsp;working some some national Indian magazines and newspaper Indian Express, he knew only hard core Capt Ajit Vadakayil will give him everything cut and dry, without mincing words.<br />\n<br />\nSo I had dinner with his family and then he gave me the poems to read.&nbsp; His wife and his 18 year old daughter were all eyes and ears. <br />\n<br />\nHalf way through, I asked the boy. \"Have you fallen in love yet , son?\" <br />\n<br />\nMy friend had already warned his family, \" With Ajit, anything can be expected. No bombshell is too big when it comes from him!\"<br />\n<br />\nThe boy said \" No , uncle \".<br />\n<br />\nSo i had my final word \" Your poems are good, but they lack intensity. I suggest you wait till you fall in love or get your first crush-- and then you will understand what I mean!. You need to polish the poems \"<br />\n<br />\nNeedless to say all were so disappointed. <br />\n<br />\nBut then this is who I am -- not very good in calling a spade a shovel.<br />\n<br />\nNow getting back--<br />\n<br />\nOne of the Engineering Superintendents was travelling to inspect a ship in USA, and he would be back after 3 days. I asked him to get a ERMETTO COUPLING from the ship's engine room workshop.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ldCzyhHEDG4/TpMaLB_f6zI/AAAAAAAAG4o/pRx4y5sDxRc/s1600/imagesCAB3NGID.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ldCzyhHEDG4/TpMaLB_f6zI/AAAAAAAAG4o/pRx4y5sDxRc/s1600/imagesCAB3NGID.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Ba2szPGG6ik/TpMaNyWeyUI/AAAAAAAAG4s/q4iu_RiFK0M/s1600/untitledbgr.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Ba2szPGG6ik/TpMaNyWeyUI/AAAAAAAAG4s/q4iu_RiFK0M/s1600/untitledbgr.png\" /></a></div><br />\nNow , an ermetto coupling is an amazing piece of engineering&nbsp;. It is a coupling which can connect two metal pipes together to handle enormous hydraulic pressures usually around 280 bars on a ship. Two bars air pressure ,&nbsp;is what you fill in your car tyre.<br />\n<br />\nUnfortunately it so transpired , that the superintendent had to travel further to another ship with an engine emergency, and he would be delayed for another 10 days.<br />\n<br />\nSo I took one of my friends , to a toy store , bought off a toy race car , paid 32 dollars for it, and then broke it up there itself and came back to the office with just the transmission, which contained the planetary gear. <br />\n<br />\nThe Chink shop keeper and my friend were looking at me as if I was crazy. <br />\n<br />\nI am sure both would not understand what a PLANETARY GEAR means -- or the amount of intelligence which has gone into its invention.<br />\n<br />\nThen I came back to my cabin in office and did some real creative work. <br />\n<br />\nEvery time my work stuttered I would play around with the planetary gear, and this was the laughing stock of the office--Ajit deriving inspiration from some bullshit toy car gears.<br />\n<br />\nNow let me talk about technology--<br />\n<br />\nMy first encounter with planetary gears was on A class ships of SCI, made in Warnemunde , Germany , which had heavy Valle derricks and Jumbo derrick , which had planetary gear in them-- this was in the seventies. <br />\n<br />\nSince nobody understood this high tech system, there used to be lot of derrick damages, with naive officers putting gear in neutral without parking the super heavy boom. <br />\n<br />\nAt that time I remember telling myself-- these gears are meant for the next century and that too in race cars-- not on ship's lifting gear, meant to be operated by simple sailors.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0n-YuXvVkWs/TpMRGqi112I/AAAAAAAAG4Q/rM3G5uXm-kE/s1600/planetarygearset.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"312\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0n-YuXvVkWs/TpMRGqi112I/AAAAAAAAG4Q/rM3G5uXm-kE/s320/planetarygearset.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\nSee the picture above--<br />\n<br />\nThe black OUTER GEAR is RING GEAR<br />\nThe green &nbsp;CENTRE GEAR is SUN GEAR<br />\nThe three yellow INTERMEDIATE GEARS are called PLANETARY GEARS.<br />\n<br />\nYou hold one gear stationary, input drive power into the second gear and take output drive torque from the third--as simple as that. And you can choose which to hold stationary which to input and which to take output from , as per your choice.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-MbmusfcXdho/TpMSaTGJCGI/AAAAAAAAG4U/m65TC36giKw/s1600/plantarygearsetgearchart.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-A-gzbwU4774/TpR7lTF2w1I/AAAAAAAAG5g/r91je4qjwIQ/s1600/imagesCAJYLI4H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-A-gzbwU4774/TpR7lTF2w1I/AAAAAAAAG5g/r91je4qjwIQ/s1600/imagesCAJYLI4H.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">We had racism all over the world, but this takes the cake. Read and understand what went on in my home state of Kerala for 6000 years.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Namboodiris form a very minuscule percentage of Kerala\u2019s population today less than 0.188%.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>These Aryan Indians arrived from the Saraswati river region ( near Indus ) 6000 years ago, after a tectonic shift caused the river to be non-perennial. They walked along the west coast of India till they reached Kerala. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">At that time the local Dravidian population of Kerala worshipped nature, and they lived in harmony. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Qd3vE33uEoY/TpLBCO5tKwI/AAAAAAAAG4E/wFhHhMLcOaU/s1600/imagesCA2IRJKF.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Qd3vE33uEoY/TpLBCO5tKwI/AAAAAAAAG4E/wFhHhMLcOaU/s1600/imagesCA2IRJKF.jpg\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Namboodiris&nbsp;came along with Lord Parashurama, who was the Guru of Guru Dronacharya, who in turn was the Guru of the Pandavas and Kauravas of Mahabharata epic. Parashurama , considered an avatar of Vishnu, was a fierce warrior saint and was the great grandson of Brighu rishi. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He was the youngest of the 5 children of Jamagdhani and Renuka. One day King Sahsrarjuna killed his father. Seeing his mother totally distraught, he flew into a terrible rage and killed Sahsrarjuna and all his sons <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>swore to kill every Kshatriya of the clan. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Continuing in the vein of frenzy, he started chasing and killing every warrior ( who was not married) &nbsp;of the Kshatriya clan , with his battle axe, till his grandfather Richeek Rishi stopped him.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aXLvMJU4LKs/TpIMQOzZtLI/AAAAAAAAG2w/MunZNpaKP9g/s1600/imagesCAEICMK6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aXLvMJU4LKs/TpIMQOzZtLI/AAAAAAAAG2w/MunZNpaKP9g/s1600/imagesCAEICMK6.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Above --an Antharjanam with marakuda , wending her way to the temple.</span></em><br />\n<em><br /></em>\n<em><br /></em>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LLnhkMF9Nds/TpLBHYseBbI/AAAAAAAAG4I/FDZSTHBhiGk/s1600/untitledbhu.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"280\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LLnhkMF9Nds/TpLBHYseBbI/AAAAAAAAG4I/FDZSTHBhiGk/s320/untitledbhu.png\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lord Parashurama accompanied the Namboodiri Brahmins and came to Kerala, seized all lands and donated it to them. The term \u201cParashurama threw his axe and reclaimed Kerala from the Arabian sea\u201d must be read in this context. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;Parashurama re-claimed the land from the original landowners.&nbsp; He has NOT thrown his axe and created&nbsp;a tsunami.&nbsp; </span>Nobody dared oppose Lord Parashurama or get on his wrong side. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sOC3_b4MiDo/TpKf_BTEHxI/AAAAAAAAG3E/ihRI2DBpQHA/s1600/asd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sOC3_b4MiDo/TpKf_BTEHxI/AAAAAAAAG3E/ihRI2DBpQHA/s1600/asd.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The Namboodiris who studied the Vedas and knew Sanskrit, had their tails up and they devised the most bizarre and cruel social system on earth. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The 8000 year old Vedic caste system of Sanatana Dharma was called Chaturvarna, or a 4 tiered system for team dynamics. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It was graded inequality to sustain society in a harmonious manner \u2014 Brahmins ( knowledge , spiritual matters ) , Kshatriyas ( executive matters and defence ) , Vaishyas ( skilled workers and traders ) , Sudras ( unskilled labourers ). <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IlnIJnkTzm0/TpK57DB4IfI/AAAAAAAAG3o/gz5opYGsdlI/s1600/imagesCAODEVEI.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IlnIJnkTzm0/TpK57DB4IfI/AAAAAAAAG3o/gz5opYGsdlI/s1600/imagesCAODEVEI.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; Everybody cannot be Captains. There are various grades including navigators, engineers, crew, cooks etc\u2014every body has a role so that the ship runs smoothly in a optimum manner . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The wages are not the same. He drove away the Thiyyas. He then donated all lands to the newly formed class, Namboodiris- who would geminate and produce their own Kshatriya Nair class. The ordinary people of Kerala suffered from Vishnu\u2019s two avatars. Vamana &nbsp;avatar who killed the beloved Asura king ( Thiyyas were the Asuras ) Mahabali and later Parashurama , to grab the lands and donate it to Namoodiris.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\">During the reign of\nKing Vikramaditya in 7000 BC, the people of Kerala called Thirayyar ( sea warriors\n) did trade with the Island of Crete. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">The patron saint of the\nKerala Thirayyars &nbsp;is &nbsp;Rishi Therayar , the first disciple of Maharishi\nAgastya . A Namboodiri woman can never marry a Nair man or have sex with him. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">If a married Namboodiri girl has sex with another namboodiri or a Nair she is excommunicated after a most elaborate 6 stage trial termed smarthavicharam. The first stage is daasi vicharam (the trial of the maidservant ) in which a prima facie report is taken from the maid of the suspected Antharjanam's sexual misdeeds or lack of mental chastity. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;Personal affections are placed on the back burner. </span>If there is prima facie evidence (sangayum thurumbum), the Antharjanam is isolated, anchampurayilackal (isolating the accused in a special cell) - the second stage.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>After the woman is isolated, the head of the family informs the ruler about the trial, and the king sends four lawyers, together with a smarthan (the judge) and Brahmin representative of the king. The lawyers, in consultation with the representatives of the king, prepare the questions. The third stage involves questioning by the smarthan regarding the status of the accused as a Antharjanam. The smarthan questions her sitting outside of her cell without seeing her. </span></span></i><br />\n<br />\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">The questioning will continue for several sessions - sometimes for several days - until the accused accepts the allegations and becomes a Saathanam or is proved innocent. The accused woman is subjected to physical torture during this time. A popular method was to pack the guilty woman in a pullupaya mat, like a dead body, and roll it from the housetop. Other women were also forced to carry out torture to make the accused confess her guilt.&nbsp; Rats,&nbsp;snakes and scorpions&nbsp;were driven into the isolation cell of the Saathanam. </span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">It must be remembered that those close blood relatives living under the same roof until the woman became an accused undertook such inhuman types of torture. The literal meaning of Saathanam is inanimate object. A Saathanam loses her status as an Antharjanam, and the smarthan questions the Saathanam face to face to get the names of the jaarans (the men involved). </span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">It was not enough that the Saathanam names the jaarans, but she had to prove it, specifying some body mark in the private parts of the man thus named. The trial would continue until the smarthans are convinced there aint no more jaarans. The king would be informed of the men involved in the offence.&nbsp; If the accused men denied the accusation, they were subjected to sathiyapariksha (a test of truth) at a Suchidran temple to prove their innocence. </span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">The fourth stage is sorupamchollal: if the accused men are found innocent through the test, they are declared innocent. The fifth stage is dehavichedam in which the Saadhanam, as well as the involved guilty men, are ceremoniously excommunicated. In the sixth stage, sudhabhojanam (pure meal), there is a sharing of a meal among the accused and the trial team once the accused is proved innocent. </span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">The last reported smarthavicharam took place in 1918, but the most famous was the samarthvicharam of Kuriyedath Dhatri. This is the period when a man demonstrates SELF RESTRAINT .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nWhen the scriptural studies appropriate to the student have been completed, and he has received blessings of his Guru, let him enter into the order of the Grihastha (householder). Let him pursue and obtain, by ethical ways, home, wife, children and wealth, discharge to the best of his ability the duties of his life's stage.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n\u2014\u2009Vishnu Purana, 3.IX.1 - 3.IX.31 5000 BC</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIT IS THE LYING WHITE INVADER WHO MADE PRESERVATION OF SEMEN , AND BEING UNMARRIED AS A GREAT QUALIFICATION IN HINDUISM \u2013 SANATANA DHARMA BANS IT . .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIN GRIHASTA STAGE THE MAN IS NOT ALLOWED TO HAVE SEX WITH ANY WOMAN WHO COMES HIS WAY , LIKE HOW THE NAMBOODIRIS DID IN KERALA ( SAMBANDHAM ) .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nHE CAN HAVE SEX ONLY WITH HIS WIFE AND CONTINUING HIS LINEAGE IS PART OF HIS DHARMA .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nThe 7000 year old Vedas lay down that dharma performed by a man alone without his wife is no dharma and will yield no fruit whatsoever. Such is the paramount nature of Grihasta ashrama.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nThe Vedas hold marriage to be one of the important sacraments sanctifying the body. That is why; marriage is given great importance by the Hindus.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIt is said, \u201cThat man who does not win a wife is really half, and he is not the full man as long as he does not beget an offspring.\u201d A wife is also hailed as\u201d the very source of the Purusharthas, not Only of Dharma, Artha and Kama but even of Moksha.\u2019</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nEvery Hindu god had his wife almost as a part of him, not as a shadow.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nShiva is powerless without Shakti.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nMarriage in Sanatana Dharma is NOT for sexual pleasure.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nEvery Hindus man is compulsorily expected to undergo the \u201cvivaha samskara\u201d and run a family (kutumba). Never mind what FREEMASON and Jew Rothschild\u2019s UNMARRIED Vivekananda said .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: medium;\">Vedas ordain that dharma must be practiced by man together with his wife.</span></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIn Sanatana Dharma, marriage is a religious duty, and not a civil contract. It is regarded as one of the most sacred of the sacraments symbolizing the holy and indissoluble union of a couple who thereafter are mutually dependent and indispensable in the performance of religious duties.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nProgeny instrumental to cementing a relationship and for bliss.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: medium;\"><b>Manu Smriti clearly states that \u201che is a perfect man, who consists of his wife, himself and his offspring.\u201d</b></span><br />\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nVedas have enjoined that dharma must be observed by man together with his wife. No yagna performed or pilgrimages undertaken will have any effect, if the wife is not a partner in those holy duties during the grihasta and vanaprasta ashramas. During Sanyasa the man can go for pilgrimage on his own.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nThe early shastras permit unmarried girls to take the whole responsibility upon themselves of choosing their life-mates and enter into wedlock with them. They need to wait for three years only after puberty for some responsible elder to arrange for their marriage, but no more.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIn Sanatana Dharma marriages are made in heaven , NOT by LIVING IN TOGETHER ( like in the west ) and examining if the wife can indeed give him a good blow job whenever he wants it\u2014</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n--or vice versa--</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nif the husband can use his tongue power on her fungi affected , smelling like putrid fish part whenever she wishes .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nMy own marriage was arranged.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nMy elder son\u2019s marriage was arranged</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIN OUR FAMILY THERE HAS NEVER EVER BEEN CAESARIAN BIRTHS \u2013THOUGH INDIA WAS THE FIRST TO DO THIS SURGICAL PROCEDURE.</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIT WAS ROTHSCHILD MEDIA AND HISTORIANS WHO GAVE UNWARRANTED PROPAGANDA FOR UNMARRIED HINDU GURUS ( I AM SURE YOU KNOW WHO THEY ARE ) .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nA LOT OF THESE UNMARRIED FAKE GURUS WERE CRYPTO JEW HOMOSEXUALS - -- OR JUST FAKE AND BACKDATED CREATIONS OF THE WHITE INVADER - THEY ARE HEROES IN YOUR NCERT TEXT BOOKS .</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nIt is the white invader who wrote lies that Hindus ill treat women and suppress them. AND THAT YUDDHISTRA STILL\nHAS SEEDS OF EGO WITHIN HIMS WHICH MAKES HIM UNFIT FOR MOKSHA ..<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nYAMAs EXPLANATION: WHOEVER KRISHNA KILLED --ALL GOT MOKSHA\n.. THERE IS NO SHORT CUT OR\nJUGAAD POSSIBLE-- LIKE ROTHSCHILDs CREATION BABAJI ( OR SOME RASCAL LIKE SRI\nSRI RAVISHANKAR ) GIVING YOU DEEKSHA .<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nREMEMBER WE ARE ALL IMMORTAL. WE ALL WERE BORN WITH THE\nSTARS .<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nYOU , YOUR GREAT GRANDFATHER AND YOU WOULD BE GREAT GRANDSON\nWERE ALL BORN AT THE SAME SPLIT SECOND.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nVISHNU AVATARS WERE NOT BORN WITH THE STARS LIKE YOU AND ME\n. THEIR SOULS WERE CREATED AND SENT DOWN FOR A PURPOSE ON EARTH.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nAFTER THEIR MISSION ON EARTH WAS OVER , THEIR SOULS MERGED\nBACK TO BRAHMAN ON SEVENTH ASTRA LAYER ( VAIKUNTA ).<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nIT IS IMPOSSIBLE FOR CON-MEN TO CLAIM THAT THEY ARE\nDESCENDANTS OF RAMA OR KRISHNA..<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nALL MORTALS ON EARTH LIKE YOU AND ME --WERE BORN WITH THE\nSTARS--THE SAME SPLIT SECOND<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nTHIS MEANS YOUR GREAT GRANDFATHER, YOU AND YOUR GREATGRANSON\nWAS BORN AT THE SAME SPILT SECOND.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nWE WERE ALL PART OF THE MOTHER FIELD NAMED BRAHMAN ON THE\nSEVENTH ASTRAL LAYER<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nTHIS IS WHY HINDUS DO NAMASTE\u2014WE HONOUR THE PIECE OF BRAHMAN\nWITHIN THE OTHER PERSON.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nTHE GOD OF SANATANA DHARMA IS A \"MORHOGENETEIC\nCONSCIOUSNESS FIELD- BRAHMAN \" WHICH CANNOT HE PICKED UP BY THE 5\nSENSES--ON MICRO AND MACRO SCALE.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nON MICRO SCALE THIS EMPTY SPACE ( INTELLIGENT FIELD )\nPROVIDES PERPETUAL MOTION WITHIN AN ATOM.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nhttp://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2016/12/perpetual-motion-of-orbiting-electrons.html<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nON MACRO SCALE IT IS AKASHA ( ETHER ) WHERE THE ENTIRE\nCOSMOS HOLDS THEIR POSITIONS<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nIn Dvaita Hinduism opposite poles Tamas and Rajas are\nconscious of each other. Tamas creates Rajas, and Rajas activates/ excites\nTamas. Sattva preserves and mediates .<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n7000 year old Vedas say that the only constant in the cosmos\nis change, everything is in a state of flux, nothing is static-- everything is\nvibratory. This is what guarantees growth and evolution. It is a cosmic\nspiraling dance of separate opposing forces, which sustains this universe<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nOne cannot exist without the other and they are dependant .\nNo phenomenon in this universe is completely devoid of its opposite. They\nconsume each other yet support each other.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nIf the restraining balance or equilibrium is lost by the\nmediator ( Vishnu ) , the universe will spiral out of control and end. This is\nwhy Lord Vishnu is called the PRESERVER god. And only Vishnu can have mortal\navatars.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nAs for the opposing forces TAMAS/ RAJAS ( Brahma/ Shiva ) it\nreally does NOT matter as who is who, like in AC electricity-where you can plug\ninto the socket both ways.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThese two opposing forces are natural and transform each\nother , in perfect harmony. Harmony can never be stagnant . Lessening of Tamas\nalways results in increase of Rajas and vice versa.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nBalance can never be permanent\u2014 Tamas and Rajas continiously\ndevour each other \u2013 and life flows on. This universe cannot exist without\nvibrations between two poles.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nTHE THIRD TEMPLATE IS SAMKHYA<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nCONTINUED TO 5-<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nCapt. Ajit VadakayilAugust 13, 2018 at 7:48 AM<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nCONTINUED FROM 4--<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThis is about the male and female joint TEAM effort. This is\nNOT a dance of opposites. In Hinduism we call the MALE- purusha and FEMALE-\nprakriti.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nIn the Tantric cosmology, the whole universe is perceived as\nbeing created, penetrated and sustained by two fundamental forces, which are\npermanently in a perfect, indestructible UNION. These forces or universal\naspects are called Shiva ( Purusha ) and Shakti (Prakriti ).<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nEach of the trinity gods are powerless without their\nconsorts.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nPurusha and Pragati is expressed as Shiva and Shakti in the\nsame body 50:50 \u2013 this is NOT a she boy or a transgender . It is a\nmindboggling, intelligent concept.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nBoth Shiva and Shakti are Consciousness---- Shiva is the\nchangeless static aspect of Consciousness, and Shakti is the kinetic, active\naspect of the same Consciousness.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThrough uniting with Purusha , Pragati gave form to his\nspirit and created the universe.(we are talking about CREATION OF THE COSMOS\nhere- not street side sex as figured out by small minds)<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nWhen the insentient Prakriti comes in contact with the\nsentient Purusha , the universe evolves.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nPurusha symbolizes consciousness, the masculine principle.\nPragati symbolizes the feminine principle, the activating energy.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThe cosmos in all its manifestations, as an act of love. The\nrelationship between say- Shakti and Shiva is the dance of consciousness and\nenergy<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nPrakriti cannot be perceived, not because of its\nnon-existence, but because of its subtlety. It is perceived in its effects.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThe eternal and indestructible union between Shiva and\nShakti gives birth to the whole Macrocosm, in its stable, static aspect as well\nas in its dynamic one. Not only is Shakti responsible for creation, it is also\nthe agent of all change<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nShakti is manifested by Shiva only during creation and is\nwithdrawn into himself at the end of creation. This is for the perceptive.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nModern science repeats from our Vedas that matter and energy\nare interchangeable. MAHABALI WAS BANISHED BY VISHNU AVATAR VAMANA TO PATALA ( PERU ) WHICH WAS PART OF HIS OWN KINGDOM..</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">THE SANSKRIT , ASTRONOMY AND MATH KNOWING CREAM OF THIYYAS WERE KERALA NAMBOODIRIS..&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">KERALA NAMBOODIRIS PROPAGATED THE VEDAS ORALLY FOR 330 CENTURIES ( THE GREATEST FEAT OF MAN ) BEFORE THEY WERE PENNED DOWN 70 CENTURIES AGO AT THE BANKS OF THE SARASWATI RIVER..</span></div>\n<div style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px;\">\n<b><span style=\"color: blue;\">KERALA NAMBOODIRIS ( ELDEST BROTHERS ) ARE THE ARYANS WITH SWASTIKA SYMBOL&nbsp;</span></b>AND SPECIAL HAIRDO..&nbsp; CHANAKYA , ADI SHANKARACHARYA , ARYABHATTA , VARARUCHI , APOLLONIUS OF TYANA ( ON WHOM JESUS CHRIST WAS MODELED ), JETHRO ( ON WHOM MOSES WAS MODLLED ) ETC WERE KERALA NAMBOODIRIS..</div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">THE&nbsp;</span><b style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">YOUNGER BROTHERS OF KERALA NAMBOODIRIS WERE THE SEMITES&nbsp;WITH SIX POINTED STAR AS SYMBOL</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">.. MOHAMMAD THE PROPHET, WAS A SEMITE WHOSE FATHERs ELDER BROTHER WAS THE NAMBOODIRI PRIEST OF THE SHIVA TEMPLE AT MECCA OASIS. THE DISGRACES LEFT HANDED SEMITES CREATED JUDAISM AND RIGHT TO LEFT HEBREW..</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">AFTER GERMAN JEW ROTHSCHILD STARTED RULING INDIA, THIYYAS WERE DEMOTED AND CONVERTED TO TODDY TAPPING MONKEYS ..</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">BE VERY VERY VERY CLEAR-- THIYYAS ( THIRAYYARS ) ARE NOT BLUNT FACED EZHAVAS (MALAYYAR TRIBALS ) WHICH WHOM THEY HAVE BEEN CLUBBED TODAY BY THE WHITE INVADER..&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">NO THIYYA WILL EVER GIVE HIS DAUGHTER / SON TO AN EZHAVA ( SOUTH OF THRISSUR ) FOR MARRIAGE, THOUGH MARRIAGE BUREAUS CLUB THEM IN THE SAME BASKET....&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">THE GLORY OF DANAVA CIVILIZATION WAS SUNK BY THE WHITE MAN AND WE WERE PAINTED AS SAVAGES..</span><br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px;\">\n<b><span style=\"color: purple;\">WHY DID VISHNU AVATAR PARASHURAMA GIVE KERALA NAMBOODIRIS SPECIAL POWERS ?..&nbsp;</span></b></div>\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: purple; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-weight: 700;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: purple; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold;\">MAIN REASON WAS ORAL TRANSMISSION OF VEDAS MUST CONTINUE, THERE MUST BE NO SUBDIVISION AND FRAGMENTATION OF FERTILE LAND ( ONLY ELDEST BROTHER OF KERALA NAMBOODIRIS COULD OWN LAND ) TO PRODUCE GOLDEN MEAN HOLY TOPSOIL FOOD AND AYURVEDIC HERBS..</span><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\"><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/07/king-cobra-and-snake-temples-of-kerala.html</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">NAMBOODIRIS GOT DRUNK WITH POWER AND THEY STARTED ILL TREATING THIYYA KINGS ( WHO MUST KEEP 6 FEET AWAY ) ..&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">ADI SHANKARACHARYA A KERALA NAMBOODIRI GOT EXASPERATED AND DISTRIBUTED THE 4 VEDAS TO THE 4 CORNERS OF INDIA, 4000 YEARS AGO, BUT WITH A FIAT THAT ALL THE 4 MUTTS MUST BE HEADED BY A KERALA NAMBOODIRI..</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">CONTINUED TO 2--</span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-INUWPzxNu4o/TpAUy2BTGjI/AAAAAAAAG2c/wMBbtHmHzk8/s1600/A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"240\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-INUWPzxNu4o/TpAUy2BTGjI/AAAAAAAAG2c/wMBbtHmHzk8/s320/A.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"><strong>ADIOS STEVE JOBS--<span style=\"color: blue;\">WHY CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL DOES NOT USE APPLE PRODUCTS-- </span><span style=\"color: magenta;\">CONFLICT BLOOD MINERALS SOURCED BY APPLE FROM CONGO</span></strong></span><br />\n<br />\nTwo days ago Steve Jobs passed away due to Cancer.&nbsp; Eulogies -nay -elegies are still pouring in.<br />\n<br />\nI must opine that , yes--&nbsp; INNOVATOR and showman Steve Jobs made his mark on this planet, with his army of genius worker drones --&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n-- <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">but he is the dirt under the&nbsp;finger nail of&nbsp; INVENTOR Nikola Tesla who made a dent in the universe, single handedly</span>. <br />\n<br />\nWe must not lose track of reality here.<br />\n<br />\nSteve Jobs backpacked and travelled&nbsp;to India by the usual Hippie trail, as a 18 year old , with his friend Dan Kottke ( who was the first employee at Apple ) in 1974. The hippie movement had fizzed out in India by that time. <br />\n<br />\nHippies were non-violent young Westerners from USA and Europe, who were anti-establishment, and believed in simple living, peace, love for beauty and large hearted giving . Today we have the information super highway afforded by internet and Google and Apple due to these un-selfish hippies.<br />\n<br />\nSteve Jobs went back to USA as a Buddhist and a vegetarian . He used to wear loose Indian clothes, and would fast once in a while. He also experimented with LSD.&nbsp; His marriage in 1991 was solemnised by a Buddhist monk.<br />\n<br />\nWhile in India he got thrashed royally by a near mob for insulting a cow. &nbsp;So goodbye nostalgia!<br />\n<br />\nI am reminded of an incident 20 years ago, when my ship's agent in one of the US ports told me that he had been to India, including Mumbai . So I asked him to name one street in Mumbai. He gave me the name of a Police station&nbsp;in Mumbai and he said he was imprisoned there for one night. <br />\n<br />\nIt so transpired that a cow sat in the middle of the road, creating a huge traffic jam. So our man gets frisky, gets down from his cab, walks up to the cow happily sitting and chewing cud , and gives one resounding kick on her poor backside.&nbsp; Needless to say all onlookers were aghast-- and since he appeared to be too smug about his singular&nbsp;deed , he had to cool his heels in the police lock up for one night. Or the policemen would have got lynched.<br />\n<br />\nI told him \" Who the fuc# told you to kick a holy Indian cow in India , and that too in front of a crowd-- serves you right, for being a moron ! \"&nbsp; and we both had a huge laugh.<br />\n<br />\nProbably the royal thrashing by a mob, the death of his chosen Guru just&nbsp;before he arrived in India, and acute dysentry which he picked up-- made him lose India in the blind sector of his radar. India would never ever come up again in his script. Till he died he treated India like a pariah market, unlike his competition who pro-actively wooed India. <br />\n<br />\nI would say, India gave him answers which \" flew in the wind!\" .&nbsp; Bob Dylan , another American Hippie of the sixties wrote a classic song on this theme.<br />\n<br />\nIronically the day&nbsp;he died , India took out her answer to I Pad. A fabulous touch tablet computer for just 35 US dollars , 15 times cheaper than Apple's cheapest model. Now why is this statement so dang important? Coz Steve Jobs made sure apple products are priced more in India that the rich West. <br />\n<br />\nI know this because I bought a I phone for my son in Chennai. When my son moved to USA, he left his apple I-phone behind, as it will NOT work in USA. For every small addition he had to use his credit card and download the program from the net. These are all hidden costs. You cant even back up your IPod on your computer.<br />\n<br />\nI dont use that phone, despite it obvious high tech features and smooth finger touch screen. For the same reason I dont drink Starbucks coffee. Steve Jobs knew very well about the conflict minerals ( tungsten, gold, tantalum ) from Congo. He could have done something for that desperately poor nation. Bill Gates has done a lot for charity-right?&nbsp; Yes, 1/3 of his wealth. Bill gates made his products cheap and accessible to the poor third world, right? This is the meaning of being human. <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nSteve Job's motivating \"read out from a paper\" speech at Stanford University USA, in 2005, &nbsp;is below. I still wonder if he was such a genius , why could he not do it extempore.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/D1R-jKKp3NA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/D1R-jKKp3NA&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/D1R-jKKp3NA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">QUOTE </span>: <span style=\"font-size: large;\">Your time is limited, so don\u2019t waste it living someone else\u2019s life.
